```
  - lib/decompress.c:decompress_method
  - lib/earlycpio.c:find_cpio_data
Direct callers:
  - lib/string.c:bcmp
```
**Symbols:**

```
ffffffff81acfa20-ffffffff81acfa45: memcmp (STB_GLOBAL)
```
</details>
</li>
</ul>
